max_ngram_size - 1, num_embed_table_per_ngram), int32.\n\n    Returns:\n        Offsets of shape (num_ngram_layers, (max_ngram_size - 1) * num_embed_table_per_ngram), int32.\n    \"\"\"\n engram_hash_ref(\n    ngram_token_ids: torch.Tensor,\n    multipliers: torch.Tensor,\n    vocab_sizes: torch.Tensor,\n    offsets: torch.Tensor,\n) -> torch.Tensor:\n    \"\"\"Pure PyTorch reference implementation of engram hash.\n\n    Args:\n        ngram_token_ids: N-gram token IDs of shape (num_tokens, max_ngram_size), int32.\n        multipliers: Per-layer hash multipliers of shape (num_ngram_layers, max_ngram_size), int64.\n        vocab_sizes: Per-layer per-ngram embedding table sizes of shape\n            (num_ngram_layers, max_ngram_size - 1, num_embed_table_per_ngram), int32.\n        offsets: Per-layer embedding table offsets of shape\n            (num_ngram_layers, (max_ngram_size - 1) * num_embed_table_per_ngram), int32.\n\n    Returns:\n        Embedding indices of shape (num_ngram_layers, num_tokens, (max_ngram_size - 1) * num_embed_table_per_ngram), int32.\n    \"\"\"\n    num_ngram_layers = multipliers.shape[0]\n    max_ngram_size = multipliers.shape[1]\n\n    prod = ngram_token_ids.to(torch.int64).unsqueeze(0) * multipliers.unsqueeze(1)\n\n    ans = [[] for _ in range(num_ngram_layers)]\n    hashes = prod[:, :, 0].clone()\n    for i in range(1, max_ngram_size):\n        hashes.bitwise_xor_(prod[:, :, i])\n        for layer_idx in range(num_ngram_layers):\n            ans[layer_idx].append((hashes[layer_idx].unsqueeze(-1) % vocab_sizes[layer_idx, i - 1].to(torch.int64).unsqueeze(0)).to(torch.int32))\n\n    for layer_idx in range(num_ngram_layers):\n        ans[layer_idx] = torch.cat(ans[layer_idx], dim=-1)\n\n    output torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:\n    \"\"\"Pure PyTorch reference implementation of engram gate (vectorized, supports autograd).\n\n    Computes: output = x + sigmoid(signed_sqrt(dot(RMSNorm(x, wh), hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16.\n        If save_for_backward is True: tuple of (output, dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k).\n    \"\"\"\n    hidden_size = hidden_states.shape[-1]\n    scalar = blk_d\n    reduce_blk = threads * vec_size\n    sub_blks = blk_d // reduce_blk\n    v_start_phase = num_blk % 2\n\n    @T.prim_func\n    def engram_gate_fwd_kernel(\n        hidden_states: T.StridedTensor[(num_tokens, hidden_size), (v_stride_s, 1), T.bfloat16],\n        weight_fused: T.Tensor[(hc_mult, hidden_size), T.float],\n        output: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), T.bfloat16],\n        dot_out: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult), T.float],\n        gate_score: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult), T.float],\n        rstd_x: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult), T.float],\n        rstd_k: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult), T.float],\n    ):\n        with T.Kernel(hc_mult, num_persistent_blocks, threads=threads) as (pid_h, pid_b):\n            thread_idx = T.get_thread_binding()\n            x_local = T.alloc_local((vec_size,), T.float)\n            k_local = T.alloc_local((vec_size,), T.float)\n            w_local = T.alloc_local((vec_size,), T.float)\n            v_local = T.alloc_local((vec_size,), T.float)\n            gate_score_local = T.alloc_local((1,), T.float)\n            rstd_x_local = T.alloc_local((1,), T.float)\n            rstd_k_local = T.alloc_local((1,), T.float)\n            gate_score_reducer = T.alloc_local((1,), T.float)\n            rstd_x_reducer = T.alloc_local((1,), T.float)\n            rstd_k_reducer = T.alloc_local((1,), T.float)\n\n            x_smem = T.alloc_shared((hidden_size,), T.bfloat16)\n            kv_smem = T.alloc_shared((2, blk_d), T.bfloat16)\n\n            per_block = T.ceildiv(num_tokens, num_persistent_blocks)\n            t_start = T.min(per_block * pid_b, num_tokens)\n            t_end = T.min(per_block * (pid_b + 1), num_tokens)\n\n            for i_s in T.Serial(t_start, t_end):\n                # === Pass 1: Reduction with cp.async pipeline ===\n                if i_s == t_start:\n                    T.async_copy(hidden_states[i_s, pid_h, 0:blk_d], x_smem[0:blk_d])\n                    T.async_copy(k[i_s, pid_h, 0:blk_d], kv_smem[0, :])\n\n                T.clear(rstd_k_local)\n                T.clear(rstd_x_local)\n                T.clear(gate_score_local)\n\n                for i_b in T.Serial(1, num_blk):\n                    phase = i_b % 2\n                    prev_phase = (i_b - 1) % 2\n                    T.async_copy(hidden_states[i_s, pid_h, i_b * blk_d:(i_b + 1) * blk_d], x_smem[i_b * blk_d:(i_b + 1) * blk_d])\n                    T.async_copy(k[i_s, pid_h, i_b * blk_d:(i_b + 1) * blk_d], kv_smem[phase, :])\n                    T.ptx_wait_group(2)\n                    for i_sub in T.Serial(sub_blks):\n                        sub_base = (i_b - 1) * blk_d + i_sub * reduce_blk\n                        for i_k in T.vectorized(vec_size):\n                            x_local[i_k] = x_smem[sub_base + thread_idx * vec_size + i_k]\n                            k_local[i_k] = kv_smem[prev_phase, i_sub * reduce_blk + thread_idx * vec_size + i_k]\n                        for i_k in T.vectorized(vec_size):\n                            w_local[i_k] = weight_fused[pid_h, sub_base + thread_idx * vec_size + i_k]\n                        for i_k in T.serial(vec_size):\n                            rstd_x_local[0] += x_local[i_k] * x_local[i_k]\n                            rstd_k_local[0] += k_local[i_k] * k_local[i_k]\n                            gate_score_local[0] += x_local[i_k] * w_local[i_k] * k_local[i_k]\n\n                # Epilogue: process last tile\n                T.ptx_wait_group(0)\n\n                # Prefetch v[0] into freed kv_smem bank\n                T.async_copy(v[i_s, 0:blk_d], kv_smem[v_start_phase, :])\n\n                for i_sub in T.Serial(sub_blks):\n                    sub_base = (num_blk - 1) * blk_d + i_sub * reduce_blk\n                    for i_k in T.vectorized(vec_size):\n                        x_local[i_k] = x_smem[sub_base + thread_idx * vec_size + i_k]\n                        k_local[i_k] = kv_smem[(num_blk - 1) % 2, i_sub * reduce_blk + thread_idx * vec_size + i_k]\n                    for i_k in T.vectorized(vec_size):\n                        w_local[i_k] = weight_fused[pid_h, sub_base + thread_idx * vec_size + i_k]\n                    for i_k in T.serial(vec_size):\n                        rstd_x_local[0] += x_local[i_k] * x_local[i_k]\n                        rstd_k_local[0] += k_local[i_k] * k_local[i_k]\n                        gate_score_local[0] += x_local[i_k] * w_local[i_k] * k_local[i_k]\n\n                # Prefetch v[1]\n                T.async_copy(v[i_s, blk_d:2 * blk_d], kv_smem[1 - v_start_phase, :])\n\n                rstd_k_reducer[0] = T.warp_reduce_sum(rstd_k_local[0])\n                rstd_x_reducer[0] = T.warp_reduce_sum(rstd_x_local[0])\n                gate_score_reducer[0] = T.warp_reduce_sum(gate_score_local[0])\n\n                rstd_x_reducer[0] = T.rsqrt(rstd_x_reducer[0] / hidden_size + eps)\n                rstd_k_reducer[0] = T.rsqrt(rstd_k_reducer[0] / hidden_size + eps)\n\n                if save_for_backward:\n                    if thread_idx == 0:\n                        dot_out[i_s, pid_h] = gate_score_reducer[0]\n                        rstd_x[i_s, pid_h] = rstd_x_reducer[0]\n                        rstd_k[i_s, pid_h] = rstd_k_reducer[0]\n\n                gate_score_reducer[0] = gate_score_reducer[0] * rstd_x_reducer[0] * rstd_k_reducer[0] * scalar\n\n                gate_score_reducer[0] = T.sigmoid(T.copysign(T.sqrt(T.clamp(T.abs(gate_score_reducer[0]), clamp_value, float('inf'))), gate_score_reducer[0]))\n\n                if save_for_backward:\n                    if thread_idx == 0:\n                        gate_score[i_s, pid_h] = gate_score_reducer[0]\n\n                # === Pass 2: Output — x from smem, v from kv_smem (tiles 0,1 already prefetched) ===\n                for i_b in T.Serial(num_blk):\n                    tile_phase = (v_start_phase + i_b) % 2\n                    if i_b < num_blk - 1:\n                        T.ptx_wait_group(1)\n                    else:\n                        T.ptx_wait_group(0)\n                        # Prefetch next token's k and x\n                        if i_s + 1 < t_end:\n                            T.async_copy(k[i_s + 1, pid_h, 0:blk_d], kv_smem[0, :])\n                            T.async_copy(hidden_states[i_s + 1, pid_h, 0:blk_d], x_smem[0:blk_d])\n                    for i_sub in T.Serial(sub_blks):\n                        sub_base = i_b * blk_d + i_sub * reduce_blk\n                        for i_k in T.vectorized(vec_size):\n                            x_local[i_k] = x_smem[sub_base + thread_idx * vec_size + i_k]\n                            v_local[i_k] = kv_smem[tile_phase, i_sub * reduce_blk + thread_idx * vec_size + i_k]\n                        for i_k in T.vectorized(vec_size):\n                            output[i_s, pid_h, sub_base + thread_idx * vec_size + i_k] = x_local[i_k] + gate_score_reducer[0] * v_local[i_k]\n                    # Prefetch v[i_b+2] into freed kv_smem bank\n                    if i_b + 2 < num_blk:\n                        T.async_copy(v[i_s, (i_b + 2) * blk_d:(i_b + 3) * blk_d], kv_smem[tile_phase, :])\n\n    return engram_gate_fwd_kernel\n\n\n@tilelang.jit(\n    pass_configs={\n        tilelang.PassConfigKey.TL_DISABLE_WARP_SPECIALIZED: True,\n        tilelang.PassConfigKey.TL_DISABLE_THREAD_STORAGE_SYNC: True,\n        tilelang.PassConfigKey.TL_DISABLE_OUT_OF_BOUND_WARNING: True,\n    },\n)\ndef get_engram_gate_bwd_kernel(\n    hidden_size: int,\n    scalar: float,\n    k_stride_s: int,\n    k_stride_h: int,\n    v_stride_s: int,\n    num_persistent_blocks: int,\n    clamp_value: float = 1e-6,\n    hc_mult: int = 4,\n):\n    \"\"\"Backward kernel: 8 warps per CTA, 2 warps per head.\n\n    grad_out and v cached in shared memory. grad_w accumulates in registers.\n    Cross-warp dldg reduction via shared memory.\n    \"\"\"\n    assert hc_mult == 4\n    num_tokens = T.dynamic('num_tokens')\n    warp_size = 32\n    warps_per_head = 2\n    num_warps = hc_mult * warps_per_head\n    threads = warp_size * num_warps\n    threads_per_head = warp_size * warps_per_head\n    assert hidden_size % threads == 0\n    elems_per_thread = hidden_size // threads\n    elems_per_warp_pair = hidden_size // threads_per_head\n    go_vec_size = 8\n    x_vec_size = 4\n\n    # NOTE Performance only tuned for hidden_size in {4096, 7168}\n    def _choose_v_vec_size(elems_per_thread):\n        for vec in [4, 2, 1]:\n            if elems_per_thread % vec == 0:\n                return vec\n\n    def _choose_go_blk_d(hidden_size, go_tile):\n        \"\"\"Largest multiple of go_tile that divides hidden_size, with >= 2 tiles.\"\"\"\n        result = go_tile\n        for blk in range(go_tile, hidden_size // 2 + 1, go_tile):\n            if hidden_size % blk == 0:\n                result = blk\n        return result\n\n    def _choose_x_blk_d(hidden_size, x_tile, hc_mult, warps_per_head):\n        \"\"\"Largest multiple of x_tile that divides hidden_size, <= hidden_size // 2, fits in smem.\"\"\"\n        smem_fixed = (hc_mult + 1) * hidden_size * 2 + hc_mult * warps_per_head * 4\n        smem_per_x = 2 * hc_mult * (2 + 2 + 4)\n        x_smem_limit = (get_max_smem_per_sm() - smem_fixed) // smem_per_x\n        x_limit = min(x_smem_limit, hidden_size // 2)\n        result = x_tile\n        for blk in range(x_tile, x_limit + 1, x_tile):\n            if hidden_size % blk == 0:\n                result = blk\n        return result\n\n    v_vec_size = _choose_v_vec_size(elems_per_thread)\n    go_blk_d = _choose_go_blk_d(hidden_size, threads_per_head * go_vec_size)\n    x_blk_d = _choose_x_blk_d(hidden_size, threads_per_head * x_vec_size, hc_mult, warps_per_head)\n\n    assert hidden_size % go_blk_d == 0 and hidden_size % x_blk_d == 0\n    assert go_blk_d % (threads_per_head * go_vec_size) == 0\n    assert x_blk_d % (threads_per_head * x_vec_size) == 0\n    assert go_blk_d + x_blk_d <= hidden_size\n\n    def smem_layout(i, j, vs):\n        thread_id = i * threads_per_head + (j // vs) % threads_per_head\n        local_id = (j % vs) + (j // (threads_per_head * vs)) * vs\n        return thread_id, local_id\n\n    @T.prim_func\n    def engram_gate_bwd_kernel(\n        grad_out: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), T.bfloat16],\n        hidden_states: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), T.bfloat16],\n        k: T.StridedTensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), (k_stride_s, k_stride_h, 1), T.bfloat16],\n        v: T.StridedTensor[(num_tokens, hidden_size), (v_stride_s, 1), T.bfloat16],\n        weight_fused: T.Tensor[(hc_mult, hidden_size), T.float],\n        dot_in: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult), T.float],\n        gate_in: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult), T.float],\n        rstd_x_in: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult), T.float],\n        rstd_k_in: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult), T.float],\n        grad_x: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), T.bfloat16],\n        grad_k: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), T.bfloat16],\n        grad_v: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hidden_size), T.bfloat16],\n        grad_w_partial: T.Tensor[(num_persistent_blocks, hc_mult, hidden_size), T.float],\n    ):\n        with T.Kernel(num_persistent_blocks, threads=threads) as pid_p:\n            tid = T.get_thread_binding()\n            warp_id = T.get_warp_idx()\n            lane_id = T.get_lane_idx()\n            head_id = warp_id // warps_per_head\n            sub_warp_id = warp_id % warps_per_head\n\n            go_local = T.alloc_local((go_vec_size,), T.float)\n            v_local = T.alloc_local((go_vec_size,), T.float)\n            go_v_local = T.alloc_local((v_vec_size,), T.float)\n            go_x_local = T.alloc_local((x_vec_size,), T.float)\n            x_local = T.alloc_local((x_vec_size,), T.float)\n            k_local = T.alloc_local((x_vec_size,), T.float)\n            w_fused_local = T.alloc_local((x_vec_size,), T.float)\n            grad_v_partial = T.alloc_local((v_vec_size,), T.float)\n            grad_w_local = T.alloc_local((elems_per_warp_pair,), T.float)\n\n            dldg_local = T.alloc_local((1,), T.float)\n            dldg_r = T.alloc_local((1,), T.float)\n\n            gate_local = T.alloc_local((hc_mult,), T.float)\n            gate_local_hc = T.alloc_var(T.float)\n            rstd_x_local = T.alloc_var(T.float)\n            rstd_k_local = T.alloc_var(T.float)\n            dot_in_local = T.alloc_var(T.float)\n            dot_x_local = T.alloc_var(T.float)\n            dot_k_local = T.alloc_var(T.float)\n\n            go_copy_layout = T.Fragment((hc_mult, go_blk_d), forward_fn=partial(smem_layout, vs=go_vec_size))\n            x_copy_layout = T.Fragment((hc_mult, x_blk_d), forward_fn=partial(smem_layout, vs=x_vec_size))\n\n            go_smem = T.alloc_shared((hc_mult, hidden_size), T.bfloat16)\n            v_smem = T.alloc_shared((hidden_size,), T.bfloat16)\n            x_smem = T.alloc_shared((2, hc_mult, x_blk_d), T.bfloat16)\n            k_smem = T.alloc_shared((2, hc_mult, x_blk_d), T.bfloat16)\n            w_smem = T.alloc_shared((2, hc_mult, x_blk_d), T.float)\n            dldg_smem = T.alloc_shared((hc_mult, warps_per_head), T.float)\n\n            per_block = T.ceildiv(num_tokens, num_persistent_blocks)\n            t_start = T.min(per_block * pid_p, num_tokens)\n            t_end = T.min(per_block * (pid_p + 1), num_tokens)\n\n            T.clear(grad_w_local)\n\n            for i_s in T.serial(t_start, t_end):\n                # === Prologue: load grad_out and v into smem ===\n                if i_s == t_start:\n                    T.async_copy(v[i_s, :], v_smem)\n                    T.async_copy(grad_out[i_s, :, :go_blk_d], go_smem[:, :go_blk_d], loop_layout=go_copy_layout)\n                    T.ptx_wait_group(1)\n                    # ensure v_smem is readable by all threads\n                    T.sync_threads()\n\n                T.copy(gate_in[i_s, :], gate_local)\n\n                # Per-head scalar loads\n                gate_local_hc = gate_in[i_s, head_id]\n                rstd_x_local = rstd_x_in[i_s, head_id]\n                rstd_k_local = rstd_k_in[i_s, head_id]\n                dot_in_local = dot_in[i_s, head_id]\n\n                T.clear(dldg_local)\n\n                go_sub_blks = go_blk_d // (threads_per_head * go_vec_size)\n                num_go_tiles = hidden_size // go_blk_d\n\n                # === Pass 1a: dldg — two warps per head ===\n                for i_b in T.serial(1, num_go_tiles):\n                    T.async_copy(grad_out[i_s, :, i_b * go_blk_d:(i_b + 1) * go_blk_d],\n                                 go_smem[:, i_b * go_blk_d:(i_b + 1) * go_blk_d],\n                                 loop_layout=go_copy_layout)\n                    T.ptx_wait_group(1)\n                    for i_sub in T.serial(go_sub_blks):\n                        go_base = (i_b - 1) * go_blk_d + i_sub * threads_per_head * go_vec_size + sub_warp_id * warp_size * go_vec_size\n                        for i_k in T.vectorized(go_vec_size):\n                            go_local[i_k] = go_smem[head_id, go_base + lane_id * go_vec_size + i_k]\n                            v_local[i_k] = v_smem[go_base + lane_id * go_vec_size + i_k]\n                        for i_k in T.serial(go_vec_size):\n                            dldg_local[0] += go_local[i_k] * v_local[i_k]\n\n                # Epilogue: process last go tile\n                T.ptx_wait_group(0)\n                for i_sub in T.serial(go_sub_blks):\n                    go_base = (num_go_tiles - 1) * go_blk_d + i_sub * threads_per_head * go_vec_size + sub_warp_id * warp_size * go_vec_size\n                    for i_k in T.vectorized(go_vec_size):\n                        go_local[i_k] = go_smem[head_id, go_base + lane_id * go_vec_size + i_k]\n                        v_local[i_k] = v_smem[go_base + lane_id * go_vec_size + i_k]\n                    for i_k in T.serial(go_vec_size):\n                        dldg_local[0] += go_local[i_k] * v_local[i_k]\n\n                # Cross-warp dldg reduction via smem\n                dldg_local[0] = T.warp_reduce_sum(dldg_local[0])\n                if lane_id == 0:\n                    dldg_smem[head_id, sub_warp_id] = dldg_local[0]\n                T.sync_threads()\n\n                # Prefetch next token's v\n                if i_s + 1 < t_end:\n                    T.async_copy(v[i_s + 1, :], v_smem)\n\n                T.async_copy(hidden_states[i_s, :, :x_blk_d], x_smem[0, :, :], loop_layout=x_copy_layout)\n                T.async_copy(k[i_s, :, :x_blk_d], k_smem[0, :, :], loop_layout=x_copy_layout)\n                T.async_copy(weight_fused[:, :x_blk_d], w_smem[0, :, :], loop_layout=x_copy_layout)\n\n                # Gate derivative\n                dldg_r[0] = dldg_smem[head_id, 0] + dldg_smem[head_id, 1]\n                dldg_r[0] = T.Select(\n                    T.abs(dot_in_local) * scalar * rstd_x_local * rstd_k_local < clamp_value,\n                    0.0,\n                    dldg_r[0] * gate_local_hc * (1.0 - gate_local_hc) * 0.5 * T.sqrt(scalar * rstd_x_local * rstd_k_local / T.abs(dot_in_local))\n                )\n\n                # === Pass 1b: grad_v ===\n                for i in T.serial(elems_per_thread // v_vec_size):\n                    T.clear(grad_v_partial)\n                    for i_h in T.unroll(hc_mult):\n                        for i_k in T.vectorized(v_vec_size):\n                            go_v_local[i_k] = go_smem[i_h, i * threads * v_vec_size + tid * v_vec_size + i_k]\n                        for i_k in T.vectorized(v_vec_size):\n                            grad_v_partial[i_k] += go_v_local[i_k] * gate_local[i_h]\n                    for i_k in T.vectorized(v_vec_size):\n                        grad_v[i_s, i * threads * v_vec_size + tid * v_vec_size + i_k] = grad_v_partial[i_k]\n\n                dot_x_local = dot_in_local * rstd_x_local * rstd_x_local / hidden_size\n                dot_k_local = dot_in_local * rstd_k_local * rstd_k_local / hidden_size\n\n                # === Pass 2: grad_x, grad_k, grad_w — pipelined x/k, 2 warps per head ===\n                x_sub_blks = x_blk_d // (threads_per_head * x_vec_size)\n                num_x_tiles = hidden_size // x_blk_d\n\n                for i_b in T.unroll(1, num_x_tiles):\n                    phase = i_b % 2\n                    prev = (i_b - 1) % 2\n\n                    T.async_copy(hidden_states[i_s, :, i_b * x_blk_d:(i_b + 1) * x_blk_d],\n                                 x_smem[phase, :, :], loop_layout=x_copy_layout)\n                    T.async_copy(k[i_s, :, i_b * x_blk_d:(i_b + 1) * x_blk_d],\n                                 k_smem[phase, :, :], loop_layout=x_copy_layout)\n                    T.async_copy(weight_fused[:, i_b * x_blk_d:(i_b + 1) * x_blk_d],\n                                 w_smem[phase, :, :], loop_layout=x_copy_layout)\n\n                    T.ptx_wait_group(3)\n\n                    for i_sub in T.unroll(x_sub_blks):\n                        sub_off = i_sub * (threads_per_head * x_vec_size) + sub_warp_id * (warp_size * x_vec_size)\n                        global_base = (i_b - 1) * x_blk_d + sub_off\n                        reg_base = ((i_b - 1) * x_sub_blks + i_sub) * x_vec_size\n                        for i_k in T.vectorized(x_vec_size):\n                            go_x_local[i_k] = go_smem[head_id, global_base + lane_id * x_vec_size + i_k]\n                            x_local[i_k] = x_smem[prev, head_id, sub_off + lane_id * x_vec_size + i_k]\n                            k_local[i_k] = k_smem[prev, head_id, sub_off + lane_id * x_vec_size + i_k]\n                            w_fused_local[i_k] = w_smem[prev, head_id, sub_off + lane_id * x_vec_size + i_k]\n                        for i_k in T.vectorized(x_vec_size):\n                            grad_x[i_s, head_id, global_base + lane_id * x_vec_size + i_k] = \\\n                                go_x_local[i_k] + dldg_r[0] * (k_local[i_k] * w_fused_local[i_k] - x_local[i_k] * dot_x_local)\n                            grad_k[i_s, head_id, global_base + lane_id * x_vec_size + i_k] = \\\n                                dldg_r[0] * (x_local[i_k] * w_fused_local[i_k] - k_local[i_k] * dot_k_local)\n                        for i_k in T.serial(x_vec_size):\n                            grad_w_local[reg_base + i_k] += dldg_r[0] * x_local[i_k] * k_local[i_k]\n\n                # Epilogue: process last x/k/w tile + prefetch next token's go\n                T.ptx_wait_group(0)\n\n                # ensure v_smem is ready and go_smem[:go_blk_d] is clean\n                T.sync_threads()\n                if i_s + 1 < t_end:\n                    T.async_copy(grad_out[i_s + 1, :, :go_blk_d], go_smem[:, :go_blk_d], loop_layout=go_copy_layout)\n\n                for i_sub in T.unroll(x_sub_blks):\n                    sub_off = i_sub * (threads_per_head * x_vec_size) + sub_warp_id * (warp_size * x_vec_size)\n                    global_base = (num_x_tiles - 1) * x_blk_d + sub_off\n                    reg_base = ((num_x_tiles - 1) * x_sub_blks + i_sub) * x_vec_size\n                    for i_k in {"type":"reasoning","timestamp":1784463576326,"sessionID":"ses_085afa16bffeNR0bMvsdqfaS8N","part":{"id":"prt_f7a50b7c9001IK7FkX3kFPjuhD","messageID":"msg_f7a50b54f001CGdsnXsp32EuME","sessionID":"ses_085afa16bffeNR0bMvsdqfaS8N","type":"reasoning","text":"Now I have a good understanding. Let me think about the algorithm:\n\nInputs (at grader params: num_tokens=8192, hc_mult=4, hidden_size=4096):\n- hidden_states: (8192, 4, 4096) bfloat16 = 256 MB\n- k: (8192, 4, 4096) bfloat16 = 256 MB\n- v: (8192, 4096) bfloat16 = 64 MB\n- weight_fused: (4, 4096) float32 = 64 KB\n\nOutputs:\n- output: (8192, 4, 4096) bfloat16 = 256 MB\n- dot: (8192, 4) float32 = 128 KB\n- gate_score: (8192, 4) float32 = 128 KB\n- rstd_x: (8192, 4) float32 = 128 KB\n- rstd_k: (8192, 4) float32 = 128 KB\n\nTotal bytes (save mode): 256*2 + 64 + 0.064 + 256 + 0.5 ≈ 832 MB\nSo the lower bound is 832 MB / time. At ~5 TB/s peak HBM bandwidth on MI350, the minimum time would be about 166 us.\n\nWait, MI350 has high bandwidth. Let me look up. MI300X has 5.3 TB/s, MI350 (gfx950) should be similar or slightly more. Let me actually measure it.\n\nThe algorithm per (token, head):\n- rstd_x = rsqrt(mean(x^2) + eps)\n- rstd_k = rsqrt(mean(k^2) + eps)\n- raw_dot = sum(x * k * weight_fused)\n- dot = raw_dot * rstd_x * rstd_k * scalar\n- gate = sigmoid(signed_sqrt(clamp_min(|dot|, clamp_value), dot.sign))\n- out = x + gate * v (v shared across heads)\n\nThis is memory-bandwidth bound. The biggest wins come from minimizing memory traffic and maximizing achieved HBM bandwidth.\n\nKey observations:\n1. We read x and k once (they're huge, can't fit in cache)\n2. We read v once per token (it's shared across all 4 heads)\n3. We need to compute x + gate*v which writes back x's shape\n\nMemory traffic in the fused version (reading x, k, v, w, writing out, dot, gate, rstd_x, rstd_k):\n- x: 8192*4*4096*2 = 256 MB (read once)\n- k: 8192*4*4096*2 = 256 MB (read once)\n- v: 8192*4096*2 = 64 MB (read once)\n- w: 4*4096*4 = 64 KB (read once, fits in L2)\n- out: 256 MB (write once)\n- dot/gate/rstd_x/rstd_k: 4 * 8192*4*4 = 128 KB each (small)\n\nTotal: ~832 MB\n\nThe TileLang kernel does this in 2 passes: pass 1 reduces x^2, k^2, x*k*w; pass 2 computes output x + gate*v. Looking at the TileLang kernel more carefully, it uses `T.Kernel(hc_mult, num_persistent_blocks, threads=32)` - so it has hc_mult * num_persistent_blocks programs. Each program handles a fixed head and a chunk of tokens (persistent). The v is read by each program for its assigned tokens, but in pass 2 only.\n\nActually, when v_start_phase and \"Prefetch v[i_b+2]\" - they prefetch v tiles and reuse the kv_smem bank that previously held k. So v is loaded once per (program, token) = once per (head, token).\n\nOK so the TileLang kernel reads v 4x (once per head). With 64MB of v and 4 reads = 256 MB of v traffic. Plus 256 MB each of x, k, output. Total 1.04 GB. But the benchmark reports 873 MB. So they only count v once (since it's only counted in the bytes count, not actual traffic).\n\nSo my Triton kernel can be even faster by reading v only once per token (across all 4 heads). That would save 192 MB of HBM traffic, bringing total to 640 MB.\n\nHmm but that's at most a 640/873 = 0.73x improvement. Plus the TileLang kernel may be L2-cached for v.\n\nLet me actually look at what speedup we need: TileLang 615us, target < 246us.\n\nLet me design my Triton kernel:\n\nOption A: One program per (token, head)\n- Pros: simple, parallelism = 32768 programs\n- Cons: v is read 4x per token\n\nOption B: One program per token (handle all 4 heads)\n- Pros: v read once per token\n- Cons: more registers/smem needed; parallelism = 8192 programs (still plenty for 256 SMs)\n\nFor hidden_size=4096, total smem per program in Option B:\n- v: 8 KB (bf16)\n- For each head (4 total), but processed sequentially: x (8KB), k (8KB) -> 16 KB reused\n- weight_fused: maybe stream it\nTotal: ~24 KB, fits easily\n\nBut wait, if we process all 4 heads sequentially in one program, we have to load v once but the loads of x and k are the same total. And we'd reuse v across the 4 heads in smem.\n\nLet me start with Option A first (simpler), then optimize to Option B if needed.\n\nActually, let me think about what would be the best for MI350's architecture. MI350 (gfx950) has:\n- 256 SMs (Compute Units)\n- 256 KB L0 (per CU) - actually I should verify this\n- 4 MB L2 cache\n- HBM3e with ~5.3 TB/s (or 8 TB/s) bandwidth\n\nThe key for bandwidth is good vectorization (128-bit loads/stores) and coalescing.\n\nTriton on ROCm has good support for vectorized loads. Let me write the kernel.\n\nActually let me try a different approach: \n\nFor each (token, head) program:\n- Hidden size = 4096\n- Use BLOCK_D = 4096 (one tile per program) - this is a single tile\n- num_warps = 8 (256 threads), each thread handles 16 elements\n- Or num_warps = 4 (128 threads), each thread handles 32 elements\n\nWith BLOCK_D = 4096, the kernel:\n1. Load x_ptrs (4096 bf16) -> x tensor\n2. Load k_ptrs (4096 bf16) -> k tensor\n3. Load w_ptrs (4096 fp32) -> w tensor (cached in L2 since it's 16KB per head)\n4. Compute sum_x2 = tl.sum(x * x)\n5. Compute sum_k2 = tl.sum(k * k)\n6. Compute raw_dot = tl.sum(x.to(fp32) * k.to(fp32) * w)\n7. rstd_x = rsqrt(sum_x2 / H + eps)\n8. rstd_k = rsqrt(sum_k2 / H + eps)\n9. dot = raw_dot * rstd_x * rstd_k * scalar\n10. abs_dot = max(abs(dot), clamp_value)\n11. signed_sqrt = sqrt(abs_dot) * sign(dot)\n12. gate = sigmoid(signed_sqrt)\n13. Load v_ptrs (4096 bf16) -> v\n14. out = x.to(fp32) + gate * v.to(fp32)\n15. Store out as bf16\n16. If save: store dot, gate, rstd_x, rstd_k to scalars\n\nFor the reduction, tl.sum should work fine on a 4096-element tensor with 256 threads.\n\nNow, the issue is: keeping x in registers across the reduction (sum) and the output computation. Triton's compiler should handle this, but the x tensor (4096 bf16 = 8KB) might end up in SMEM if it doesn't fit in registers.\n\nEach thread handles 16 elements. If we keep them as fp32 in registers, that's 16 fp32 = 64 bytes = 16 registers per thread. Total: 16 * 256 = 4096 registers, which is fine.\n\nLet me try this approach.\n\nActually wait, there's a subtlety. The reference does:\n- raw_dot = sum(x * wh, k * we)\n- which equals sum(x * k * wh * we) = sum(x * k * weight_fused)\n\nSo the math is:\n- raw_dot = sum over d of (x[d] * k[d] * weight_fused[h, d])\n- dot = raw_dot * rstd_x * rstd_k * scalar\n- gate = sigmoid(signed_sqrt(clamp_min(|dot|, clamp_value)))\n- out = x + gate * v\n\nFor numerical accuracy matching the reference, we need to:\n- Use float32 for the multiplications and reductions\n- The reference does x.float() and k.float() first, so I should upcast\n\nLet me check the calc_diff metric. It's:\n```\nsim = 2 * (x * y).sum() / (x * x + y * y).sum()\nreturn 1 - sim\n```\n\nThis is a relative L2 distance. Need < 2e-10, which is very tight. So I need to match the reference closely.\n\nFor the reduction order, the reference does it in float32, summing in some order. Triton's tl.sum uses a tree reduction which may give slightly different order. With float32 sums of 4096 elements, the differences should be tiny but might exceed 2e-10 in the dot product.\n\nActually, let me check: calc_diff is computed in double precision. So we're comparing fp32 results bit-by-bit-ish.\n\nHmm, 2e-10 is quite tight. Let me check if Triton's reduction can achieve this. Actually since the result is sigmoid(... sqrt(...)), small differences in dot get attenuated. Let me just try and see.\n\nLet me also verify the eps. The test uses eps = 1e-20 which is very small. So rstd is essentially 1/sqrt(mean(x^2)).\n\nLet me write the kernel and test it.\n\nActually wait, let me think about the reduction accuracy more carefully. The reference computes:\n- raw_dot = torch.einsum('...d,...d->...', x * wh, k * we)\n- This is essentially: sum over d of (x[d] * wh[d] * k[d] * we[d])\n\nWhen wh * we = weight_fused, this is sum over d of (x[d] * k[d] * weight_fused[d]).\n\nFor numerical equivalence, I should compute it as:\n- raw_dot = sum(x_fp32 * k_fp32 * weight_fused)\n\nBut the reference computes it as:\n- (x * wh) * (k * we) summed\n- = (x * wh * k * we) summed\n\nThese should be the same up to fp32 rounding. The order of operations might differ but for the comparison threshold of 2e-10, it should be fine.\n\nActually wait, wh and we are bf16 in the reference, then converted to fp32:\n```python\nwh = weight_hidden.float().unsqueeze(0)  # bf16 -> fp32\nwe = weight_embed.float().unsqueeze(0)\nraw_dot = torch.einsum('...d,...d->...', x * wh, k_f * we)\n```\n\nSo the reference uses bf16 wh and we (cast to fp32). But our function gets weight_fused = (wh * we) in fp32 already. So if we use weight_fused directly, we get x * k * (wh * we) where (wh * we) is computed in fp32 from bf16. \n\nThe reference does (x * wh) * (k * we) which is essentially x*wh*k*we, but with possibly different rounding:\n- (wh * we) computed once: weight_fused = wh.float() * we.float() - this rounds to fp32 once\n- Then x * k * weight_fused - this is what we compute\n\nvs reference:\n- x_fp32 * wh_fp32 = temp1 (rounded)\n- k_fp32 * we_fp32 = temp2 (rounded)\n- temp1 * temp2 (rounded)\n- sum over d\n\nThese should be very close but not bit-exact. The difference should be at most a few ULPs per element, and with 4096 elements summed, the relative error should be very small. Let me just try and verify.\n\nOK let me write the Triton kernel now.\n\n```python\nimport torch\nimport triton\nimport triton.language as tl\n\n\n@triton.jit\ndef _engram_gate_fwd_kernel(\n    X_ptr, K_ptr, V_ptr, W_ptr,\n    OUT_ptr, DOT_ptr, GATE_ptr, RSTD_X_ptr, RSTD_K_ptr,\n    stride_x_t, stride_x_h,\n    stride_k_t, stride_k_h,\n    stride_v_t,\n    stride_out_t, stride_out_h,\n    H: tl.constexpr,\n    scalar,\n    eps,\n    clamp_value,\n    HC: tl.constexpr,\n    SAVE: tl.constexpr,\n    BLOCK_D: tl.constexpr,\n):\n    # One program per (token, head)\n    pid = tl.program_id(0)\n    t = pid // HC\n    h = pid % HC\n\n    # Pointers\n    x_offset = t * stride_x_t + h * stride_x_h\n    k_offset = t * stride_k_t + h * stride_k_h\n    v_offset = t * stride_v_t\n    w_offset = h * H\n    out_offset = t * stride_out_t + h * stride_out_h\n\n    d_range = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_D)\n    mask = d_range < H\n\n    # Load x, k, w\n    x_ptrs = X_ptr + x_offset + d_range\n    k_ptrs = K_ptr + k_offset + d_range\n    w_ptrs = W_ptr + w_offset + d_range\n    v_ptrs = V_ptr + v_offset + d_range\n\n    x = tl.load(x_ptrs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n    k = tl.load(k_ptrs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n    w = tl.load(w_ptrs, mask=mask, other=0.0)\n\n    # Reductions\n    sum_x2 = tl.sum(x * x)\n    sum_k2 = tl.sum(k * k)\n    raw_dot = tl.sum(x * k * w)\n\n    rstd_x = tl.rsqrt(sum_x2 / H + eps)\n    rstd_k = tl.rsqrt(sum_k2 / H + eps)\n\n    dot = raw_dot * rstd_x * rstd_k * scalar\n\n    abs_dot = tl.abs(dot)\n    clamped = tl.maximum(abs_dot, clamp_value)\n    sqrt_val = tl.sqrt(clamped)\n    sign_dot = tl.where(dot >= 0, 1.0, -1.0)\n    signed_sqrt = sqrt_val * sign_dot\n    gate = tl.sigmoid(signed_sqrt)\n\n    # Output: out = x + gate * v\n    v = tl.load(v_ptrs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n    out = x + gate * v\n    out_bf16 = out.to(tl.bfloat16)\n\n    out_ptrs = OUT_ptr + out_offset + d_range\n    tl.store(out_ptrs, out_bf16, mask=mask)\n\n    if SAVE:\n        tl.store(DOT_ptr + t * HC + h, raw_dot)\n        tl.store(GATE_ptr + t * HC + h, gate)\n        tl.store(RSTD_X_ptr + t * HC + h, rstd_x)\n        tl.store(RSTD_K_ptr + t * HC + h, rstd_k)\n```\n\nWait, this uses BLOCK_D = H = 4096. With 256 threads (8 warps), each thread holds 16 elements. The reductions tl.sum will work via tree reduction across threads.\n\nLet me think about whether to use a larger num_warps. It comes from the reduction order in tl.sum vs torch.einsum.\n\nThe reference computes:\n```python\nraw_dot = torch.einsum('...d,...d->...', x * wh, k_f * we)\n```\n\nThis is sum over d of (x[d] * wh[d]) * (k[d] * we[d]).\n\nMy kernel computes:\n```python\nraw_dot = tl.sum(x * k * w)  # where w = weight_fused = wh * we\n```\n\nThis is sum over d of x[d] * k[d] * (wh[d] * we[d]).\n\nThe difference:\n1. Order of multiplications: (x*wh)*(k*we) vs x*k*(wh*we)\n2. The precomputed w = wh*we is rounded to fp32 once, vs wh*we computed per-element in the reference (same thing actually)\n3. Reduction order: tl.sum (tree reduction) vs torch.einsum (sequential? or also tree?)\n\nTo match exactly, I should compute (x * wh) * (k * we) - but I don't have wh and we separately!\n\nHmm. But wait - the function only receives weight_fused. So I CAN'T compute it the same way as the reference. Unless I factor weight_fused into wh and we... which is impossible without knowing the original values.\n\nSo there's an inherent discrepancy between my kernel (using weight_fused) and the reference (using wh and we separately). This discrepancy exists for TileLang too, since TileLang also only gets weight_fused.\n\nLet me check: is my dot diff the same as TileLang's dot diff? The per-token\n    value vector ``v`` is loaded once and reused across those heads, cutting\n    v HBM traffic by a factor of ``HC // HEADS_PER_PROG``.\n\n    The head and hidden dimensions are folded into a 2-D block\n    ``(HEADS_PER_PROG, BLOCK_D)`` so that loads/stores for all heads in the\n    group are issued together, giving the compiler maximum freedom to overlap\n    memory and compute.\n    \"\"\"\n    pid = tl.program_id(0)\n    num_head_groups = HC // HEADS_PER_PROG\n    t = pid // num_head_groups\n    hg = pid % num_head_groups\n\n    d_range = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_D)\n    h_offs = tl.arange(0, HEADS_PER_PROG)\n    mask = d_range < H\n    mask_2d = mask[None, :]\n\n    # The grader\nimports THIS function and compares it against both the PyTorch reference and the\nDeepSeek TileLang kernel for correctness, then times it against the TileLang\nkernel for speedup.\n\nDo NOT change the function name or signature.\n\"\"\"\nimport torch\nimport triton\nimport triton.language as tl\n\n\ndef _next_pow2(x: int) -> int:\n    p = 1\n    while p < x:\n        p <<= 1\n    return p\n\n\n@triton.jit\ndef _engram_gate_fwd_kernel(\n    X_ptr, K_ptr, V_ptr, W_ptr,\n    OUT_ptr, DOT_ptr, GATE_ptr, RSTD_X_ptr, RSTD_K_ptr,\n    stride_x_t, stride_x_h,\n    stride_k_t, stride_k_h,\n    stride_v_t,\n    stride_out_t, stride_out_h,\n    H,\n    scalar,\n    eps,\n    clamp_value,\n    HC: tl.constexpr,\n    SAVE: tl.constexpr,\n    BLOCK_D: tl.constexpr,\n    HEADS_PER_PROG: tl.constexpr,\n):\n    \"\"\"Engram gate forward kernel for AMD MI350 (gfx950).\n\n    Each program handles one token and HEADS_PER_PROG heads.  The per-token\n    value vector ``v`` is loaded once and reused across those heads, cutting\n    v HBM traffic by a factor of ``HC // HEADS_PER_PROG``.\n\n    The head and hidden dimensions are folded into a 2-D block\n    ``(HEADS_PER_PROG, BLOCK_D)`` so that loads/stores for all heads in the\n    group are issued together, giving the compiler maximum freedom to overlap\n    memory and compute.\n    \"\"\"\n    pid = tl.program_id(0)\n    num_head_groups = HC // HEADS_PER_PROG\n    t = pid // num_head_groups\n    hg = pid % num_head_groups\n\n    d_range = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_D)\n    h_offs = tl.arange(0, HEADS_PER_PROG)\n    mask = d_range < H\n    mask_2d = mask[None, :]\n\n    # v is shared across heads — load once per program, keep in L2.\n    v_ptrs = V_ptr + (t * stride_v_t) + d_range\n    v = tl.load(v_ptrs, mask=mask, other=0.0, eviction_policy='evict_last').to(tl.float32)\n\n    # Load x, k, w for all heads in the group as a 2-D tile.\n    h_vals = hg * HEADS_PER_PROG + h_offs\n    x_ptrs = X_ptr + (t * stride_x_t + h_vals[:, None] * stride_x_h) + d_range[None, :]\n    k_ptrs = K_ptr + (t * stride_k_t + h_vals[:, None] * stride_k_h) + d_range[None, :]\n    w_ptrs = W_ptr + (h_vals[:, None] * H) + d_range[None, :]\n\n    # x, k are streamed once — evict_first frees L2 for v/w reuse.\n    x = tl.load(x_ptrs, mask=mask_2d, other=0.0, eviction_policy='evict_first').to(tl.float32)\n    k = tl.load(k_ptrs, mask=mask_2d, other=0.0, eviction_policy='evict_first').to(tl.float32)\n    # weight_fused is tiny (per-head) and reused across all tokens — keep cached.\n    w = tl.load(w_ptrs, mask=mask_2d, other=0.0, eviction_policy='evict_last')\n\n    # Per-head reductions over the hidden dim.\n    sum_x2 = tl.sum(x * x, axis=1)\n    sum_k2 = tl.sum(k * k, axis=1)\n    raw_dot = tl.sum(x * k * w, axis=1)\n\n    inv_H = 1.0 / H\n    rstd_x = tl.rsqrt(sum_x2 * inv_H + eps)\n    rstd_k = tl.rsqrt(sum_k2 * inv_H + eps)\n\n    dot = raw_dot * rstd_x * rstd_k * scalar\n    abs_dot = tl.abs(dot)\n    clamped = tl.maximum(abs_dot, clamp_value)\n    sqrt_val = tl.sqrt(clamped)\n    sign_dot = tl.where(dot >= 0, 1.0, -1.0)\n    signed_sqrt = sqrt_val * sign_dot\n    gate = tl.sigmoid(signed_sqrt)\n\n    # out = x + gate * v  (v broadcast across heads)\n    out = x + gate[:, None] * v[None, :]\n    out_ptrs = OUT_ptr + (t * stride_out_t + h_vals[:, None] * stride_out_h) + d_range[None, :]\n    tl.store(out_ptrs, out.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mask_2d)\n\n    if SAVE:\n        idx = t * HC + h_vals\n        tl.store(DOT_ptr + idx, raw_dot)\n        tl.store(GATE_ptr + idx, gate)\n        tl.store(RSTD_X_ptr + idx, rstd_x)\n        tl.store(RSTD_K_ptr + idx, rstd_k)\n\n\ndef _choose_cfg(hidden_size: int, hc_mult: int):\n    \"\"\"Pick (heads_per_prog, num_warps, num_stages) tuned for MI350.\"\"\"\n    block_d = _next_pow2(hidden_size)\n\n    # heads_per_prog: reuse v across heads. 2 is the sweet spot on MI350 for\n    # hidden_size <= 4096 (balances v reuse against register pressure and\n    # SM-level parallelism). For very large BLOCK_D we fall back to 1 head per\n    # program to keep register pressure manageable.\n    if hc_mult % 2 == 0 and block_d <= 4096:\n        heads_per_prog = 2\n    else:\n        heads_per_prog = 1\n\n    # num_warps: tuned empirically per BLOCK_D / heads_per_prog combination.\n    if heads_per_prog == 2:\n        # 2-D block (2, BLOCK_D); 8 warps gives best occupancy at BLOCK_D=4096.\n        if block_d >= 4096:\n            num_warps = 8\n        else:\n            num_warps = 4\n    else:\n        # 1 head per program — fewer threads needed for the 1-D block.\n        if block_d >= 8192:\n            num_warps = 4\n        elif block_d >= 2048:\n            num_warps = 2\n        else:\n            num_warps = 4\n\n    num_stages = 1\n    return heads_per_prog, num_warps, num_stages, block_d\n\n\ndef engram_gate_fwd_triton(\n    hidden_states: torch.Tensor,   # (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    k: torch.Tensor,               # (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    v: torch.Tensor,               # (num_tokens, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    weight_fused: torch.Tensor,    # (hc_mult, hidden_size), float32  (= weight_hidden * weight_embed)\n    eps: float,\n    clamp_value: float,\n    save_for_backward: bool = True,\n):\n    \"\"\"Engram gate forward.\n\n    Computes, per (token, head):\n        rstd_x  = rsqrt(mean(x^2, dim=-1) + eps)\n        rstd_k  = rsqrt(mean(k^2, dim=-1) + eps)\n        raw_dot = sum(x * k * weight_fused, dim=-1)\n        dot     = raw_dot * rstd_x * rstd_k * hidden_size**-0.5\n        gate    = sigmoid( sign(dot) * sqrt(clamp_min(|dot|, clamp_value)) )\n        out     = (x + gate * v).bfloat16()          # v is shared across heads\n\n    Returns:\n        (output, dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k)\n        When save_for_backward is False, the last four are None and only `output`\n        is required to be correct.\n        When True, dot=raw_dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k are (num_tokens, hc_mult)\n        float32 tensors.\n    \"\"\"\n    num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size = hidden_states.shape\n    scalar = hidden_size ** -0.5\n    device = hidden_states.device\n\n    assert k.stride(-1) == 1\n    assert v.stride(-1) == 1\n    k_stride_t, k_stride_h, _ = k.stride()\n    v_stride_t, _ = v.stride()\n    x_stride_t, x_stride_h, _ = hidden_states.stride()\n\n    output = torch.empty_like(hidden_states)\n    if save_for_backward:\n        dot = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)\n        gate_score = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)\n        rstd_x = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)\n        rstd_k = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)\n    else:\n        dot = gate_score = rstd_x = rstd_k = None\n\n    heads_per_prog, num_warps, num_stages, block_d = _choose_cfg(hidden_size, hc_mult)\n\n    grid = (num_tokens * (hc_mult // heads_per_prog),)\n    _engram_gate_fwd_kernel[grid](\n        hidden_states, k, v, weight_fused,\n        output, dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k,\n        x_stride_t, x_stride_h,\n        k_stride_t, k_stride_h,\n        v_stride_t,\n        x_stride_t, x_stride_h,\n        hidden_size,\n        scalar,\n        eps,\n        clamp_value,\n        HC=hc_mult,\n        SAVE=save_for_backward,\n        BLOCK_D=block_d,\n        HEADS_PER_PROG=heads_per_prog,\n        num_warps=num_warps,\n        num_stages=num_stages,\n    )\n\n    return output, dot, gate_score, The grader\nimports THIS function and compares it against both the PyTorch reference and the\nDeepSeek TileLang kernel for correctness, then times it against the TileLang\nkernel for speedup.\n\nDo NOT change the function name or signature.\n\"\"\"\nimport torch\nimport triton\nimport triton.language as tl\n\n\ndef _next_pow2(x: int) -> int:\n    p = 1\n    while p < x:\n        p <<= 1\n    return p\n\n\n@triton.jit\ndef _engram_gate_fwd_kernel(\n    X_ptr, K_ptr, V_ptr, W_ptr,\n    OUT_ptr, DOT_ptr, GATE_ptr, RSTD_X_ptr, RSTD_K_ptr,\n    stride_x_t, stride_x_h,\n    stride_k_t, stride_k_h,\n    stride_v_t,\n    stride_out_t, stride_out_h,\n    H,\n    scalar,\n    eps,\n    clamp_value,\n    HC: tl.constexpr,\n    SAVE: tl.constexpr,\n    BLOCK_D: tl.constexpr,\n    HEADS_PER_PROG: tl.constexpr,\n):\n    \"\"\"Engram gate forward kernel for AMD MI350 (gfx950).\n\n    Each program handles one token and HEADS_PER_PROG heads.  The per-token\n    value vector ``v`` is loaded once and reused across those heads, cutting\n    v HBM traffic by a factor of ``HC // HEADS_PER_PROG``.\n\n    The head and hidden dimensions are folded into a 2-D block\n    ``(HEADS_PER_PROG, BLOCK_D)`` so that loads/stores for all heads in the\n    group are issued together, giving the compiler maximum freedom to overlap\n    memory and compute.\n    \"\"\"\n    pid = tl.program_id(0)\n    num_head_groups = HC // HEADS_PER_PROG\n    t = pid // num_head_groups\n    hg = pid % num_head_groups\n\n    d_range = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_D)\n    h_offs = tl.arange(0, HEADS_PER_PROG)\n    mask = d_range < H\n    mask_2d = mask[None, :]\n\n    # v is shared across heads — load once per program, keep in L2.\n    v_ptrs = V_ptr + (t * stride_v_t) + d_range\n    v = tl.load(v_ptrs, mask=mask, other=0.0, eviction_policy='evict_last').to(tl.float32)\n\n    # Load x, k, w for all heads in the group as a 2-D tile.\n    h_vals = hg * HEADS_PER_PROG + h_offs\n    x_ptrs = X_ptr + (t * stride_x_t + h_vals[:, None] * stride_x_h) + d_range[None, :]\n    k_ptrs = K_ptr + (t * stride_k_t + h_vals[:, None] * stride_k_h) + d_range[None, :]\n    w_ptrs = W_ptr + (h_vals[:, None] * H) + d_range[None, :]\n\n    # x, k are streamed once — evict_first frees L2 for v/w reuse.\n    x = tl.load(x_ptrs, mask=mask_2d, other=0.0, eviction_policy='evict_first').to(tl.float32)\n    k = tl.load(k_ptrs, mask=mask_2d, other=0.0, eviction_policy='evict_first').to(tl.float32)\n    # weight_fused is tiny (per-head) and reused across all tokens — keep cached.\n    w = tl.load(w_ptrs, mask=mask_2d, other=0.0, eviction_policy='evict_last')\n\n    # Per-head reductions over the hidden dim.\n    sum_x2 = tl.sum(x * x, axis=1)\n    sum_k2 = tl.sum(k * k, axis=1)\n    raw_dot = tl.sum(x * k * w, axis=1)\n\n    inv_H = 1.0 / H\n    rstd_x = tl.rsqrt(sum_x2 * inv_H + eps)\n    rstd_k = tl.rsqrt(sum_k2 * inv_H + eps)\n\n    dot = raw_dot * rstd_x * rstd_k * scalar\n    abs_dot = tl.abs(dot)\n    clamped = tl.maximum(abs_dot, clamp_value)\n    sqrt_val = tl.sqrt(clamped)\n    sign_dot = tl.where(dot >= 0, 1.0, -1.0)\n    signed_sqrt = sqrt_val * sign_dot\n    gate = tl.sigmoid(signed_sqrt)\n\n    # out = x + gate * v  (v broadcast across heads)\n    out = x + gate[:, None] * v[None, :]\n    out_ptrs = OUT_ptr + (t * stride_out_t + h_vals[:, None] * stride_out_h) + d_range[None, :]\n    tl.store(out_ptrs, out.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mask_2d)\n\n    if SAVE:\n        idx = t * HC + h_vals\n        tl.store(DOT_ptr + idx, raw_dot)\n        tl.store(GATE_ptr + idx, gate)\n        tl.store(RSTD_X_ptr + idx, rstd_x)\n        tl.store(RSTD_K_ptr + idx, rstd_k)\n\n\ndef _choose_cfg(hidden_size: int, hc_mult: int):\n    \"\"\"Pick (heads_per_prog, num_warps, num_stages) tuned for MI350.\"\"\"\n    block_d = _next_pow2(hidden_size)\n\n    # heads_per_prog: reuse v across heads. 2 is the sweet spot on MI350 for\n    # hidden_size <= 4096 (balances v reuse against register pressure and\n    # SM-level parallelism). For very large BLOCK_D we fall back to 1 head per\n    # program to keep register pressure manageable.\n    if hc_mult % 2 == 0 and block_d <= 4096:\n        heads_per_prog = 2\n    else:\n        heads_per_prog = 1\n\n    # num_warps: tuned empirically. Key factor is the effective work per\n    # program (heads_per_prog * hidden_size elements to reduce + store).\n    effective_work = heads_per_prog * hidden_size\n    if heads_per_prog == 2:\n        if effective_work >= 2 * 4096:   # hidden_size >= 4096\n            num_warps = 8\n        else:                             # smaller hidden sizes\n            num_warps = 4\n    else:\n        if block_d >= 8192:\n            num_warps = 4\n        elif block_d >= 2048:\n            num_warps = 2\n        else:\n            num_warps = 4\n\n    num_stages = 1\n    return heads_per_prog, num_warps, num_stages, block_d\n\n\ndef engram_gate_fwd_triton(\n    hidden_states: torch.Tensor,   # (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    k: torch.Tensor,               # (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    v: torch.Tensor,               # (num_tokens, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    weight_fused: torch.Tensor,    # (hc_mult, hidden_size), float32  (= weight_hidden * weight_embed)\n    eps: float,\n    clamp_value: float,\n    save_for_backward: bool = True,\n):\n    \"\"\"Engram gate forward.\n\n    Computes, per (token, head):\n        rstd_x  = rsqrt(mean(x^2, dim=-1) + eps)\n        rstd_k  = rsqrt(mean(k^2, dim=-1) + eps)\n        raw_dot = sum(x * k * weight_fused, dim=-1)\n        dot     = raw_dot * rstd_x * rstd_k * hidden_size**-0.5\n        gate    = sigmoid( sign(dot) * sqrt(clamp_min(|dot|, clamp_value)) )\n        out     = (x + gate * v).bfloat16()          # v is shared across heads\n\n    Returns:\n        (output, dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k)\n        When save_for_backward is False, the last four are None and only `output`\n        is required to be correct.\n        When True, dot=raw_dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k are assert k.stride(-1) == 1\n    assert v.stride(-1) == 1\n    k_stride_t, k_stride_h, _ = k.stride()\n    v_stride_t, _ = v.stride()\n    x_stride_t, x_stride_h, _ = hidden_states.stride()\n\n    output hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)\n        rstd_x = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=device)\n        rstd_k = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult),
